PT J
AU DORFMAN, R
AF DORFMAN, R
TI MALTHUS,THOMAS,ROBERT AND RICARDO,DAVID
SO JOURNAL OF ECONOMIC PERSPECTIVES
LA English
DT Editorial Material
AB This article will describe the enduring relationship between Thomas Malthus and David Ricardo initiated by a letter Malthus sent to Ricardo in June 1811. It was, very likely, the most remarkable and most fruitful collaboration in the history of economics. It appears that their long and intimate collaboration, and their friendship as well, thrived on their continual disputations. They were two men obsessed by a common enthusiasm, tirelessly pursuing a common goal: to understand the economy. But they did not share a common vision of the good society and thus were condemned to wrestle interminably, though remarkably fruitfully, over the roles of the social classes. Their struggles to convey to each other their views of the forces that drove their economy are an inspiring case study in both the difficulty and the possibility of human communication.
RP DORFMAN, R (corresponding author), HARVARD UNIV, POLIT ECON, CAMBRIDGE, MA 02138 USA.

PT J
AU Thakor, AV
AF Thakor, Anjan V.
TI Competitive Equilibrium with Type Convergence in an Asymmetrically
   Informed Market
SO REVIEW OF FINANCIAL STUDIES
LA English
DT Article
ID LOAN COMMITMENT CONTRACTS; INSURANCE MARKETS; ECONOMICS; MODEL
AB This article studies an asymmetric information game with "type convergence," in which, under some realizations of a common uncertainty, inducing informed agents to reveal their types through self selection by contract choke is either costly or impossible. Under other realizations, self-selection permits costless distinctions between informed agents. I obtain sufficient conditions under which contracting with options prior to the realization of the common uncertainty leads to the existence of a perfectly separating costless Nash equilibrium. Applications to variable rate loan commitments and life insurance contracting are discussed.
C1 [Thakor, Anjan V.] Indiana Univ, Bloomington, IN 47405 USA.
RP Thakor, AV (corresponding author), Indiana Univ, Sch Business, Bloomington, IN 47405 USA.
CR [Anonymous], 1986, CONSUM REP, V51, P379
   BANKS JS, 1987, ECONOMETRICA, V55, P647, DOI 10.2307/1913604
   BESANKO D, 1987, INT ECON REV, V28, P671, DOI 10.2307/2526573
   BHATTACHARYA S, 1980, Q J ECON, V95, P1, DOI 10.2307/1885346
   BOOT A, 1987, J BANK FINANC, V11, P449, DOI 10.1016/0378-4266(87)90043-4
